***vervoegen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:vervoegen.html>vervoegen</a> (24695)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:voegen.html>voegen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vervoegen.html>vervoegen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to conjugate</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">proscribed</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to join</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Some <a href = vnd.unilang:speakers.html>speakers</a> use this verb to mean "to join". Many <a href = vnd.unilang:speakers.html>speakers</a> and language organisations consider this usage nonstandard and advise <a href = vnd.unilang:speakers.html>speakers</a> to use, among other <a href = vnd.unilang:things.html>things</a>, "<a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:ver.html>ver</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:voegen.html>voegen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a>" or "<a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aansluiten.html>aansluiten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a>" instead.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">vervoeging</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verbuigen.html>verbuigen</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:vervoegen.html>vervoegen</a></b>
</p>

***verwarren.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:verwarren.html>verwarren</a> (11916)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">verwerren</i>, derived from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">werren</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to confuse, be confused</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, originally a strong verb. Analysable as <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">war</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">disorder</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>, but <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">war</i>, Middle Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">werre</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> deverbal. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">verwirren</i>. Also related with English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">war</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verwarren.html>verwarren</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to tangle</li>
<li>to confuse, confound, befuddle</li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">overgankelijk</span> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> war <a href = vnd.unilang:brengen.html>brengen</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>Met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aanwezigheid.html>aanwezigheid</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:verwarren.html>verwarren</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> controleurs <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:medewerker.html>medewerker</a>.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li>

***verwelkomen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:verwelkomen.html>verwelkomen</a> (6777)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:welkom.html>welkom</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verwelkomen.html>verwelkomen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to welcome <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to affirm or greet the arrival of someone</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***verwezen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:verwezen.html>verwezen</a> (28972)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">verwesen</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wees.html>wees</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verwezen.html>verwezen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to become orphaned</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> chiefly figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to orphan, to bereave of parents</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>May be qualified by <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:half.html>half</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:heel.html>heel</a></i> to specify the loss of one or two parents respectively.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>See the etymology of the main entry.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***verwijten.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:verwijten.html>verwijten</a> (7260)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ver-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wijten.html>wijten</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to blame</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verwijten.html>verwijten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">ditransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to blame for
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:waarom.html>Waarom</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:verwijt.html>verwijt</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a>? <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heb.html>heb</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gedaan.html>gedaan</a>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Why are you blaming <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>? I <a href = vnd.unilang:did.html>did</a> not do it!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:verwijt.html>verwijt</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:regering.html>regering</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niets.html>niets</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:onderneemt.html>onderneemt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tegen.html>tegen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:slechte.html>slechte</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:weer.html>weer</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I blame the government for not taking action against the bad weather.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The indirect object <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the one being blamed, the direct object <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> what they are being blamed for.</li></ul>
